French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">rafle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:randy.html>randy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">randier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">randiest</b>)
